<Text>The entree's here were all pretty good, but I'll say that their carne asada dishes seemed to be a bit dry. Their beans and rice also taste a bit dry, so that's a pitfall.

However, their breakfast burrito is on point the best one I've had here in San Diego. The cheese is perfectly melted, the food is distributed so you can get a taste of everything in every bite, and you can swap out the bacon for sausage (which is a big deal for me, sorry bacon lovers!)

The next amazing thing here is their fish tacos, which they're known for. Perfectly battered, doesn't taste like you're eating bread the whole time. Solid fish taco, definitely a go to place for the area.</Text><pics>None<//pics>< Resp>

<username>Erin Williams</username>< rating>

<Pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipN1liZaj4Y5WWm_69L8R1cJ7LEcfleqstWMipaR=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOWVAM2aXKr5jZC0Y5aZQ6dzKVze4d8mdPN9VFU=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPGAwzgvWhuQKGp26E4kfJa57SGOK2shsHhcmYF=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOgW1JPAQwZ27WN1D6gondE3_AI2arYL-tHw0mL=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /Pictures><Response>None</Response>< review>
I've wanted to try this restaurant, and the garlic noodles, for a long long time (decades) but I just never made it to LA/BH,  until Saturday!!! I was excited to finally have the chance. Due to traffic, I had to cancel my reservation and settle for take out. I ordered from the 'An The Go' menu: chicken roll, shaken beef, garlic noodles. The chicken rolls have a strong shrimp/fishy taste. I didnt taste or detect any actual chicken flavor. You get 4 pieces (2 rolls cut in half on the diagonal) and a dipping sauce (NOT sweet and sour). I ate 2 pieces and gave the rest to my son. The fishy taste was too much for me. The shaken beef was very good. Not $42 good, but good. The meat is super tender, cooked perfectly, and the sauce is sweet and savory. The potatoes were good but burned on the bottom. They put the salad (lettuce and halved cherry tomatoes) in a separate container with a side of dressing. The dressing tasted like balsamic with a hint of fish sauce. The garlic noodles were very tasty. Tender noodles with a strong buttery garlic flavor. I really enjoyed the noodles but they overpower anything you eat with them. Its 2 days later and I'm still eating noodles. I enjoyed the meal overall but I dont ever have to go back. My total for 3 dishes was $89. Way too much for what you get. I can check Crustacean off my list of "MUST TRY" restaurants.< /review>

<Review>Very recently reopened after months of renovation, the iconic restaurant is busier than ever. The new set up is softer, less ethnic than previous but seem to accomodate more tables.

Cleaner, softer looks and feminine contemporary designs are spotted everywhere. Menu is organized well with the classics clearly highlighted and newer menus featured and explained well by the staffs.. For us, the classics still fare the best. Avoid the beef as the medium well tasted more like well done. Complicated by the table presentation also not very guest friendly as the hot plate's supposedly 500 degrees hot.

Dessert was divine, we reordered the beignets and caramelized banana. I totally get how the restaurant could maintain so many loyal patrons over decades...they really understand that dining there would and should be a treat...</Review>< Time>

<Review>On September 27, 2020, I celebrated my birthday for a second year  at this restaurant. Not excluding I have  patronized this restaurant before the remodeling, after the remodeling, and during COOVID. When it was time to pay for my bill I payed with my  EDD card because I was on medical leave from my job because my hand was fractured hand on  May 17,2020.If anyone is on medical leave form their job they are eligible to apply for state disability to assist with loss of wages if you do not have sick pay, etc.  The waiter asked for my ID to process my card. Once again, one of the restaurants of the House of An went over and above when it comes to flavour of the dishes served.  Most of what we ordered was well worth the price from the crab puffs to the A5 wagyu.
Of course the garlic noodles and garlic crab's flavour are wonderful as always, it's just that the crab meat was not as big as they used to be. Excited to try the new restaurant upstairs which I heard is good too and owned by the same family.  Now we have two more new House of An restaurants to try in SoCal, Dalat Rose and Tiato. ü•∞<//Review>

<user_id>105234362170523652866<//user_id><Name>andrew saetern< /Name><date>1546532437400<//date><rating>5< /rating>< text>
OMG.... Crustacean Beverly Hills is fantastic. Beautiful d√©cor and incredibly delicious food. I love the koi pond below the floor. Yes, I literally wanted to sit down on top of the glass and do some Koi Watching (It's a thing, right?). Too bad my suit pants were too tight for me to bend that far down. They got lucky! It was quite a relaxing evening. The fresh flowers all over the restaurant add a great touch. I often drifted from conversation and was distracted by the smell of food coming from nearby tables.

Be sure to email or go online to book your reservation ahead of time. I'm not sure they allow walk-ins. I did see a group of 4 walk in but were unable to get a table. It was slow when we arrived, but by 8pm nearly every table was occupied. It was a cold evening, so the outdoor seating was not in use. I noticed that they have seating upstairs too.

We started with drinks. I had The Ori. Strong drink, but not sure I'd get it again. Didn't quite satisfy me. I tried my friends Daughter of the Dragon and wish I had ordered that instead. Every item we ordered was full of spices and flavors. Our first dish was the Shrimp & Lobster Dumplings. These were very good. Our other 3 items arrived together: The Cauliflower & Brussel Sprouts, An's Famous Garlic Noodles, and the Lamb. The Cauliflower/Brussel Sprouts are amazing. Crispy and cooked to perfection. While the Garlic Noodles had all the right flavors, I thought it was a bit overcooked and too soggy. Lamb was tender and served with veggies. My dinner ended with a strong cup of Cappuccino.

Crustacean is certainly not a place to go if you're looking for big portions, unless you're planning to order plate after plate. Service was great, just as expected. My water was filled several times without having to ask. Sean was our server.

Valet parking is available. However, there are several public parking garages in the area.

Will I come back? YES!</text>

< name>
Tony Sdarn<//name>
<review>Introduction:

My best friend and all his relatives raved about this place and therefore I decided to pay this place a visit with my family last weekend to celebrate my mother's birthday. Out of the things we got for the evening the following deserves special mention: famous garlic roasted Dungeness crab with a side of garlic noodles, pho soup dumplings, and tuna cigars.

Food:

Garlic roasted Dungeness crab with a side of garlic noodles:

For the garlic roasted Dungeness crab I highly recommend getting it Out of Shell because it is much more convenient for consumption. The noodles, paired with the minced crab meat is buttery, garlicky and very flavorful. The texture of the noodles is al-dente and bouncy, signs that bespoke the noodles' quality.

Pho soup dumplings:

The pork inside the dumplings is very tender and tasty. The broth accompanying the dumpling is light, flavorful, mellow and wholesome. It's something I highly recommend getting on a cold night.

Tuna cigars:

The tuna cigars are a must have when visiting Crustacean. The initial presentation is eye-catching and innovative; the cigars themselves are delightful. The cigars consist of tobiko caviar at the tip with minced tuna on the inside wrapped in a thin wafer. Normally I don't like caviar because they tend to be too salty but the tobiko caviars, surprisingly, are mild in taste. I really enjoy the taste of the minced tuna: it has a pronounced smokiness to it with hints of spiciness.

Ambiance:

Elegant and contemporary in its d√©cor.

Price:

It is reasonable considering the quality of its ingredients, culinary execution and its demographic location.

Service:

The staff is cordial and polite however they did commit a faux pas. Prior to coming I have made a reservation and the establishment understands my family and I are celebrating my mother's birthday for the evening. Upon arriving my mother is given a birthday card bearing a general message congratulating and wishing her well which we appreciate. However, by the end of the evening my mother is displeased with their service because when we arrive, a small cake bearing a lit candle is brought to the table next to us. When my mother sees that, since it is her birthday, she thought by the end of the meal the staff will bring a small cake to us as well to commemorate the event. Unfortunately the cake is never brought much to my mother's disappointment and she did complain about it for the rest of the night. To me it is carelessness if the cake were not brought by accident; if the cake were not brought deliberately because my family and I have not spent a certain amount for the evening, then it is a lack of commonsense on the staffs' and establishment's part. How much can a small cake cost? $7-$10 at most; the establishment can easily make it back with the patron's gratuity. It is not worth making patrons feel they have been treated unequally when a cake is brought to one table but not the other especially if both tables happen to be right next to each other.<//review>< rate>

I was looking for a cute place to have my birthday dinner and remembered I had this gift certificate from an event that I went to called Unforgettable Gala in December. <Name>Food Shutterbug</Name><text>Had lunch at Crustacean with some friends. They don't take reservations via Open Table so I had to call them in (if you provide an email address they will send you a confirmation).

AMBIENCE: The restaurant's dark wood interior and ceiling fans lend a colonial vibe from days past and the see-through Koi fish walkway gave it a fengshui feel. ¬†It is, however, very cramped in certain parts of the restaurant.¬†Luckily we went for an early lunch on a weekday so it felt laidback.

SERVICE: The waiter knew his stuff and we followed his recommendations for an appetizer and dessert. As for the entree, there was no question that I was going to order the Roasted Crab and Garlic Noodles.

FOOD: ¬†I'm allergic to MSG so I called the restaurant in advance to see if they use it like most Asian restaurants. ¬†I had to make a few calls because the only way I could find out was to call when the Secret Kitchen cooking staff were in. ¬†To my surprise, they don't use MSG at all! ¬†The trade off is, however, some dishes were a bit too sweet such as the GARLIC ASPARAGUS (seasonal item that the waiter recommended) and the GARLIC NOODLES. ¬†The seasoning on the famed ROASTED GARLIC CRAB was savory and provided a nice counterpoint to the sweet crab meat. Thanks to a tip from a blogger, I decided to pay an extra $5 to have the crab shelled in advance -- sometimes I'm a really clumsy eater and didn't want to risk having a crab leg fly onto my friends' laps. ¬†‚Ä®‚Ä®I really enjoyed the meal, but if I were to go back, I would accompany my meal with either a dry white wine or Chinese tea to counterbalance the sweetness of most of the dishes.

PARKING: ¬†Very difficult. ¬†There's a 2 hour free parking lot nearby, but it's always full during peak times -- day or evening. ¬†I ended up parking a block away at the metered parking garage at Camden near Santa Monica Blvd.

Very Americanized cuisine. For those looking for authentic or cutting edge food, this would probably rate less stars than what I've given here.< /text>< rate>
4</rate>
